@8212   = ~Nahal's Reckless Dweomer
(Invocation/Evocation)

Level: 1
Range: Special
Duration: Special
Casting Time: Special
Area of Effect: Special
Saving Throw: Special

This spell is the Wild Mage's ultimate last-resort spell. When cast, the Mage releases a sudden flood of wild magical energy in the hope of seizing and shaping that energy into a desired spell effect. The attempt usually fails, but something almost always occurs in the process.

To use Nahal's Reckless Dweomer simply cast it, then choose from your list of known spells. A burst of magical energy is released, which the Wild Mage will try to manipulate into the desired form. The actual effect of the spell is determined randomly by a dice roll on the Wild Surge Table (see the manual for more details).

Because the release of energy is planned by the Mage, <PRO_HISHER> level is added to the dice roll. If the result indicates success, the Mage has shaped the magical energy into the desired effect. More often than not, the effect is completely unexpected. The result might be beneficial to the Mage, or it might be completely disastrous: This is the risk the Mage takes in casting Nahal's Reckless Dweomer.《那哈莽行咒*（聚能/塑能系）

等級：1
有效距離：特殊
持續時間：特殊
施法時間：特殊
影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：特殊

這是狂亂法師的終極搏命法術。施展之後，可以瞬間釋放出大量魔法能量，排山倒海般地衝向目標。法師很難控制這股能量，但是總能形成一些影響。

施法之前，法師需先聲明想以此法術創造什麼效果，此效果必須是他能夠施展的某個法術（也就是法術書中已抄錄的法術），但不需是已經記憶的法術。聲明之後（須包含法術目標和其他條件），狂亂法師即可施展那哈莽行咒。此時會爆發一股魔法能量，狂亂法師可試圖塑造其形式，但實際的效果將隨機決定。

由於法師在釋放能量前已有準備，所以投骰結果加上<PRO_HISHER>等級，才決定狂亂波動的效果，也就是等級越高越有可能得到好結果。如果成功，法師可將魔法能量塑造成想要的形式。但是此法術很可能產生無法預期的效果，預期外的結果可能對法師有利，也可能造成災難；這就是施展那哈莽行咒的風險所在。》~

@8788   = ~Heal
(Necromancy)

Level: 6
Sphere: Healing 
Range: Touch
Duration: Permanent
Casting Time: 9
Area of Effect: 1 creature
Saving Throw: None

The very potent Heal spell enables the priest to wipe away disease and injury in the creature who receives the benefits of the spell. It completely cures all disease and blindness in the recipient and heals all points of damage suffered due to wounds or injury. It also dispels a Feeblemind spell and cures those mental disorders caused by spells or injury to the brain. Naturally, the effects can be negated by later wounds, injuries, and diseases.《痊癒術（死靈系）

等級：6
領域：醫療
有效距離：觸碰
持續時間：永久
施法時間：9
影響範圍：被碰觸的生物
豁免檢定：無

這道非常強大的痊癒術可以使牧師治癒目標生物身上的疾病和所受到的傷害。法術能夠完全治好所有的目盲或是疾病狀態，並完全恢復目標生物的生命值。此法術亦可解除弱智術的影響，治好由其他法術或腦部傷害所引起的心理不正常的舉止。當然，這法術無法預防你不再次受到傷害或者疾病的影響。》~

@9550   = ~HUMANS: Humans are the predominant race in Faerûn. Humans rule most of the significant empires and kingdoms in the Forgotten Realms. They are the most social and tolerant of races, excepting perhaps the halflings. Humans may advance as any class and are also the only race that can dual-class. Humans may not multi-class.《人類：人類是費倫世界的主要種族。人類統領著「遺忘國度」中大部分的帝國和王國。他們是最友善也最能容忍異族生物的種族，容忍度大概只亞於半身人。人類可以選擇所有的職業，也可以轉職。》~
@9551   = ~DWARVES: Dwarves are short and stocky, easily identifiable by their size and shape. They have ruddy cheeks, dark eyes, and dark hair. Dwarves tend to be dour and taciturn. They are given to hard work and care little for most humor. They enjoy beer, ale, mead, but most of all, they love gold. There are four racial divisions of dwarves within the realms: shield dwarves, gold dwarves, wild dwarves, and duergar.

Dwarves have the following traits:
– +2 bonus to Saving Throws vs. Paralysis/Poison/Death, vs. Rod/Staff/Wand, and vs. Spell, with additional bonuses based on Constitution.
– Infravision.
– +10% Open Locks, +15% Find Traps, +5% Detect Illusion, +10% Set Traps.
– +1 Constitution, -1 Dexterity, -2 Charisma.《矮人：矮人的體型矮小而壯碩，他們有著紅潤的雙頰、黝黑的雙眸及深色的頭髮。矮人通常極為頑固而沉默寡言。他們對魔法和毒素具有天生抵抗力，並擁有夜視能力，可以在黑暗中辨識物體的溫度。矮人在體質上有著特別的優勢，但卻缺乏魅力和敏捷度。世界上有四種不同的矮人，分別是鋼盾矮人、黃金矮人、野矮人和灰矮人。》~
@9552   = ~ELVES: Elves tend to be shorter and slimmer than humans. Their features are finely chiseled and delicate, and they speak in melodic tones. Elves are looked upon as being frivolous and aloof. They concern themselves with natural beauty, dancing, frolicking, and other similar pursuits. Their humor is clever, as are their songs and poetry. There are six racial divisions of elves within the realms: gold elves, moon elves, wild elves, sea elves, dark elves (drow), and winged elves (avariel).

Elves have the following traits:
– 90% resistance against charm and sleep magics.
– Infravision.
– +1 THAC0 bonus with bows, short swords, and long swords.
– -5% Open Locks, +5% Pick Pockets, +5% Move Silently, +10% Hide in Shadows.
– +1 Dexterity, -1 Constitution.《精靈：精靈比一般的人類纖瘦，五官也較為細緻。精靈給人的印象通常是孤高而與世隔離。他們認為自己天生麗質，喜好舞蹈、嬉鬧等活動，長於幽默諷刺與詩歌吟唱。他們對於魅惑術和沉睡術擁有天生抵抗力。精靈擁有夜視能力，可以在黑暗中視物，也擅於使用弓和長劍。他們天生敏捷，但體質稍差。世界上有五種精靈：黃金精靈、月精靈、海精靈、野精靈和黑暗精靈。》~
@9553   = ~GNOMES: Kin to dwarves, gnomes are noticeably smaller than their distant cousins. Gnomes, as they proudly maintain, are also less rotund than dwarves. Most have dark tan or brown skin, white hair, and rather large noses. Gnomes have lively and sly senses of humor, especially for practical jokes. They have a love for nature that is only matched by their love for gems and jewelry. There are two racial divisions of gnomes within the realms: rock gnomes and deep gnomes (svirfneblin).

Gnomes have the following traits:
– +2 bonus to Saving Throws vs. Rod/Staff/Wand and vs. Spell, with additional bonuses based on Constitution.
– Infravision.
– +5% Open Locks, +10% Find Traps, +5% Move Silently, +5% Hide in Shadows, +10% Detect Illusion, +5% Set Traps.
– +1 Intelligence, -1 Wisdom.《侏儒：侏儒和矮人算是有點親戚關係，但身高卻又比他們矮上一些。侏儒們常刻意保養，因此不像矮人那麼肥胖。大多數的侏儒擁有黝黑或是褐色的皮膚，白色的頭髮和一個大鼻子。他們天性歡樂，具有淘氣的幽默感，尤其擅長惡作劇。他們愛好自然，也喜愛珠寶財物。侏儒對魔法有天生抵抗力，並擁有夜視能力，可以在黑暗中視物。他們通常智力過人，但是智慧較差。》~
@9554   = ~HALFLINGS: Halflings are short, generally plump people, very much like small humans. Their faces are round and broad and often quite florid. Their hair is typically curly, and the tops of their feet are covered with coarse hair. Overall they prefer the comforts of home to dangerous adventuring. They enjoy good living, rough humor, and homespun tales. There are three racial divisions of halflings within the realms: the hairfoot, tallfellow, and stout.

Halflings have the following traits:
– +2 bonus to Saving Throws vs. Paralysis/Poison/Death, vs. Rod/Staff/Wand, and vs. Spell, with additional bonuses based on Constitution.
– +1 THAC0 bonus with slings.
– +5% Open Locks, +5% Find Traps, +5% Pick Pockets, +10% Move Silently, +15% Hide in Shadows.
– +1 Dexterity, -1 Strength, -1 Wisdom.《半身人：半身人是矮胖的種族，和身高較矮的人類非常相似。他們的臉又大又圓，並且相當紅潤。一般而言，半身人有著一頭卷髮，腳趾常覆蓋著雜亂的毛髮。一般而言，他們喜歡舒適的家居環境，不喜歡涉險。半身人喜歡享受生活，直率的幽默以及樸實的故事。半身人對魔法和毒素有頑強的抵抗力。他們擅長使用投石索，在黑暗中也稍微看得見東西。半身人非常敏捷，但卻沒什麼力量。世界上有三種半身人：毛腳族、高個族和矮壯族。》~
@9555   = ~HALF-ELVES: Half-elves are a mix of human and elven blood. They are handsome folk, with good features from each of their parent races. A half-elf has the curiosity, inventiveness, and ambition of their human ancestors and the refined senses, love of nature, and artistic tastes of their elven ancestors.

Half-elves have the following traits:
– 30% resistance against charm and sleep magics.
– Infravision.
– +10% Pick Pockets, +5% Hide in Shadows.《半精靈：半精靈是人類和精靈的混血。他們非常俊俏，擁有兩個種族血統上的優點。半精靈擁有人類的好奇心、創造力和野心，同時也擁有精靈的敏銳感覺，以及對大自然的熱愛和對藝術的高絕品味。半精靈對於魅惑術和沉睡術有些許的抵抗力，在黑暗中也擁有夜視能力。》~

– May wear any armor and use any weapon.
– May not exceed Specialization (two slots) in any weapon class.
– May achieve Specialization (two slots) in any fighting style.

– May use the Hide In Shadows ability while wearing no armor, leather armor, or studded leather armor.

– Alignment restricted to good.
– Hit Die: d10

Whether <PRO_HESHE> turns <PRO_HISHER> talent against innocent passersby and wealthy merchants or oppressors and monsters is a choice for the Thief to make.

CLASS FEATURES:

– May not wear armor heavier than studded leather.
– May not equip shields larger than bucklers.
– May only use the following weapons: long sword, short sword, katana, scimitar, dagger, club, quarterstaff, crossbow, shortbow, dart, sling.
– May only become Proficient (one slot) in any weapon class.
– May only become Proficient (one slot) in any fighting style.
– May distribute 25 points per level (40 at level 1) in thieving abilities: Open Locks, Pick Pockets, Find Traps, Move Silently, Hide In Shadows, Detect Illusion, Set Traps.
– Starts with base scores of 10% in Open Locks, 5% in Find Traps, 15% in Pick Pockets, 10% in Move Silently, and 5% in Hide in Shadows.
– May backstab for increased damage:
  Level 1-4: x2
  Level 5-8: x3
  Level 9-12: x4
  Level 13+: x5
– May use the Set Snare ability once per day. Gains one use at level 1 and an additional use every 5 levels thereafter.

SET SNARE: Set a trap in the chosen location when no hostile creatures are in sight. Traps grow more powerful with the Thief's level and can only be triggered by enemies.
  1st level: Deals 2d8+5 missile damage.
  11th level: Deals 2d8+5 missile damage and additionally deals 2d6 poison damage per round for the next 3 rounds.
  16th level: Deals 3d8+5 missile damage and 4d8+2 fire damage.
  21st level: Deals 3d8+5 missile damage and 20 poison damage with no save; slays target if a Save vs. Death with a +4 bonus is failed.

– Alignment restricted to any except lawful good.
– Hit Die: d6

Prime Requisites For Dual-Classing: Dexterity《盜賊：顧名思義，盜賊乃是技巧高超的偷竊者。不管出於好或壞的動機，盜賊就是盜賊，詭計多端、敏捷、神出鬼沒就是他們的特色。然而，究竟要將這些技巧用在無辜的路人，還是富商土豪或怪物身上，那就是盜賊個人的抉擇了。》~

@9603   = ~LAWFUL GOOD: Characters of this alignment believe that an orderly, strong society with a well-organized government can work to make life better for the majority of the people. To ensure the quality of life, laws must be created and obeyed. When people respect the laws and try to help one another, society as a whole prospers. Therefore, lawful good characters strive for those things that will bring the greatest benefit to the most people and cause the least harm. An honest and hard-working serf, a kindly and wise king, or a stern but forthright minister of justice are all examples of lawful good people.《守序善良：這個陣營的人物相信，規律而強大的社會和道德高尚的政府，可以讓大多數人民生活得更好。只要人們尊敬法律，並試著互相幫助，整個社會就將因此而進步。因此，守序善良陣營的人物將會朝著這個方向努力，他們會盡可能地為大多數人帶來較多的福利以及較少的傷害。他們必定信守自己的承諾。一位聰明而有智慧的國王，或是一名堅持原則公平公正的法官都是此陣營的寫照。》~
@9604   = ~LAWFUL NEUTRAL: Order and organization are of paramount importance to characters of this alignment. They believe in a strong, well-ordered government, whether that government is a tyranny or a benevolent democracy. The benefits of organization and regimentation outweigh any moral questions raised by their actions. An inquisitor determined to ferret out traitors at any cost or a soldier who never questions his orders are good examples of lawful neutral behavior.《守序中立：對這個陣營的人物而言，秩序和群組織是非常重要的。他們認同強大、井然有序的統治階層，不管這個統治階層是專制獨裁的暴君，還是安和樂利的民主政府，這些人都不在乎。對他們而言，絕對的秩序比什麼道德良知要來得重要。只要是規定，不管結果是好是壞，都必須遵行無誤。一名毫不留情拷打奸細的審問者和絕對服從命令的士兵都是很好的例子。》~
@9605   = ~LAWFUL EVIL: These characters believe in using society and its laws to benefit themselves. Structure and organization elevate those who deserve to rule as well as provide a clearly defined hierarchy between master and servant. To this end, lawful evil characters support laws and societies that protect their own concerns. If someone is hurt or suffers because of a law that benefits lawful evil characters, too bad. Lawful evil characters obey laws out of fear of punishment. Because they may be forced to honor an unfavorable contract or oath they have made, lawful evil characters are usually very careful about giving their word. Once given, they break their word only if they can find a way to do it legally, within the laws of the society. An iron-fisted tyrant and a devious, greedy merchant are examples of lawful evil beings.《守序邪惡：這個陣營的人物相信，秩序的存在是為了確認統治者的利益。他們偏好階級分明的社會型態。如果對自己有利的法律會使其他人受害，那麼很抱歉，這是沒辦法的事。守序邪惡的人會因為害怕懲罰或強權壓力而遵守法律。由於他們絕對信守自己的承諾，所以他們不會輕易地立下任何誓約。只有在符合社會規範的情況下，這些人才有可能打破誓言。執行鐵腕政治的暴君或貪婪的商人都是此陣營的寫照。》~
@9606   = ~NEUTRAL GOOD: These characters believe that a balance of forces is important, but that the concerns of law and chaos do not moderate the need for good. Since the universe is vast and contains many creatures striving for different goals, a determined pursuit of good will not upset the balance; it may even maintain it. If fostering good means supporting organized society, then that is what must be done. If good can only come about through the overthrow of existing social order, so be it. Social structure itself has no innate value to them. A baron who violates the orders of his king to destroy something he sees as evil is an example of a neutral good character.《中立善良：這個陣營的人物相信力量平衡是十分重要的事，單方面地強調秩序或混亂，是無法達到至善的。因為整個宇宙中充滿了朝著各式目標而努力的生物，所以若要追求至善，便不能破壞這種平衡，甚至得設法維持這種平衡。如果說支持社會秩序可以帶來至善，便得為之。若推翻既有的社會秩序就可以達到至善，那也必須為之。社會結構對他們來說，沒什麼重大的價值。一名違背上級命令去消滅他眼中邪惡事物的士兵，就是此陣營的例子。》~
@9607   = ~NEUTRAL EVIL: Neutral evil characters are primarily concerned with themselves and their own advancement. They have no particular objection to working with others or, for that matter, going it on their own. Their only interest is in getting ahead. If there is a quick and easy way to gain a profit, whether it be legal, questionable, or obviously illegal, they take advantage of it. Although neutral evil characters do not have the every-man-for-himself attitude of chaotic characters, they have no qualms about betraying their friends and companions for personal gain. They typically base their allegiance on power and money, which makes them quite receptive to bribes. An unscrupulous mercenary, a common thief, and a double-crossing informer who betrays people to the authorities to protect and advance himself are typical examples of neutral evil characters.《中立邪惡：這個陣營的人物只關心自己的利益。如果有可以輕鬆獲利的途徑，不管是否合法，還是有道德上的爭議，這些人都會緊抓不放。雖然中立邪惡的人沒有混亂邪惡那種「人人為己」的心態，但若遇到賣友求榮的機會，他們仍然會毫不遲疑地把握住。這些人通常為了金錢和權力與人結盟，所以相當容易賄賂。無節操的傭兵、一般盜賊、求取榮華的雙面諜等都是此陣營的例子。》~
@9608   = ~TRUE NEUTRAL: True neutral characters believe in the ultimate balance of forces, and they refuse to see actions as either good or evil. Since the majority of people in the world make judgments, true neutral characters are extremely rare. True neutrals do their best to avoid siding with the forces of either good or evil, law or chaos. It is their duty to see that all of these forces remain in balanced contention. True neutral characters sometimes find themselves forced into rather peculiar alliances. To a great extent, they are compelled to side with the underdog in any given situation, sometimes even changing sides as the previous loser becomes the winner. A true neutral Druid might join the local barony to put down a tribe of evil gnolls, only to drop out or switch sides when the gnolls are brought to the brink of destruction. He would seek to prevent either side from becoming too powerful. Clearly, there are very few true neutral characters in the world.《絕對中立：這個陣營的人物相信絕對平衡的力量，因此，他們拒絕採取任何被視為是邪惡或善良的行動。絕對中立的人會盡力避免和善良或邪惡、秩序或叛逆的力量合流。他們唯一的職責，就是讓這些力量保持完美的平衡。有時候，他們會發現自己被迫得和某個陣營結盟。為了保持平衡，這些人會刻意改變立場，和弱勢者合作。然而，當強弱勢力對換時，他們也會毫不猶豫地跟著改變立場。絕對中立的德魯伊也許會加入地方貴族獵殺豺狼人的行列，然而，當這群豺狼人即將滅族之時，他們又會轉而幫助豺狼人。這些人會避免某方勢力變成絕對強勢。不過，很顯然地，世界上絕對中立的人並不多。》~

@9746   = ~Animate Dead
(Necromancy)

Level: 3
Sphere: Necromantic
Range: 30 ft.
Duration: 8 hours
Casting Time: 9
Area of Effect: Special 
Saving Throw: None 

This spell causes a skeleton warrior to rise and serve the caster under any conditions. The type of skeleton warrior that appears depends upon the level of the priest casting the spell.
  1st – 6th: a 3 HD skeleton warrior wielding a long sword.
  7th – 10th: a 5 HD skeleton warrior wielding a long sword +1.
  11th – 14th: a 7 HD skeleton warrior wielding a bastard sword +1.
  15th and up: a 9 HD skeleton warrior wielding a two-handed sword +1.
The skeleton warrior can follow the caster, remain in an area and attack any creature entering the place, etc. It remains animated until it is destroyed in combat, 8 hours pass, or it is turned. This spell cannot be dispelled.《操縱死屍（死靈系）

等級：3
領域：死靈
有效距離：30呎
持續時間：8小時
施法時間：9
影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：無

這法術可創造出一個骷髏戰士，無條件服從施法者的任何命令。法術創造出的骷髏戰士的屬性由牧師當前的等級決定：
	1-6級：骷髏戰士的生命骰數為3，手持普通長劍
	7-10級：骷髏戰士的生命骰數為5，手持+1長劍
	11-14級：骷髏戰士的生命骰數為7，手持+1巨劍
	15級以上：骷髏戰士的生命骰數為9，手持+1雙手劍

骷髏戰士會跟隨施法者施法者，停留在一處並攻擊所有進入該區域的任何敵人等等。它會一直存在到在戰鬥中被毀滅、經過八小時或是被超度為止。這個法術不受解除魔法影響。》~

@10811  = ~CAUTION!
Dual-classing is a significant change to your character. Please be sure you have read and understand the following, as well as the description given in the manual.

Dual-classing is an ability that only humans have. It is the process by which you stop advancing in your current class and begin advancing in a second class. You will retain the benefits and abilities of the first class at its current level, but from then on you will only gain experience in the second.

In order to become dual-classed, you must be of at least 2nd level in your current class. Your character must have scores of 15 or higher in the prime requisites of your current class and scores of 17 or more in the prime requisites of the class you wish to change to. Some classes cannot be combined due to alignment conflicts or inherent restrictions. Within Baldur's Gate II: Enhanced Edition, all resulting mixes must be viable multi-class combinations as well.

Dual-class characters have much the same requirements as multi-class characters. You must abide by the restrictions of the individual classes. For example: A Mage combination cannot cast spells while wearing armor, a Thief combination cannot use thieving skills while wearing armor other than leather, and a Cleric or Druid combination cannot use weapons that their ethos does not allow.

When you gain a level, you will have the option to change to a second class, provided you have the prerequisites and do not have any alignment conflicts. Your first class becomes "inactive," and you begin again at 1st level with 0 experience points in your second class. From then on, you progress as a single-classed character in your new class. ONCE YOU HAVE CHANGED TO A SECOND CLASS, YOU CANNOT GO BACK TO THE FIRST. Your first class will forever remain at its current level.

You will be unable to use the abilities of your first class until you have attained ONE LEVEL HIGHER in your new class. For example: If you were a 10th-level Mage and switched to a Fighter, you would not be able to use your Mage abilities again until you reached 11th level as a Fighter.

IMPORTANT: The experience cap in Baldur's Gate II: Enhanced Edition is 8,000,000 points for a single character. Experience points from BOTH of a dual-classed character's classes count towards this total. Please be sure that there are sufficient points left available to allow you to progress high enough in your second class! IF YOU ARE LEVEL 14 IN YOUR CURRENT CLASS, IT IS VERY LIKELY YOU WILL NOT BE ABLE TO REACH LEVEL 15 IN A SECOND CLASS. The game will still allow you to dual if you wish, but you may not be able to access your previous class's abilities within Baldur's Gate II: Enhanced Edition. This might result in difficulty later in the game.《請注意！
轉職對你的人物來說是個重大轉變，請務必閱讀以下的說明和說明書中的解說。

轉職是只有人類才有的特殊能力。在轉換成第二個職業的過程中，你的第一個職業將停止進展，只有第二個職業的經驗值能加以提升。你仍可以保有第一個職業的相關技巧和能力，但只有第二個職業能繼續升級。
人物要轉職，第一個職業的等級至少必須為第二級，而第一個職業的主要屬性至少必須在15點或以上，第二個職業的主要屬性至少必須在17點或以上。由於職業上的衝突和陣營相斥，有些職業是無法相互轉職的。在柏德之門中，所有的轉職群組合都必須是兼職可以容許的群組合。

轉職人物在許多方面和兼職人物一樣受到限制。舉例來說：轉職群組合中若有法師職業，該人物便無法穿著盔甲施法。盜賊則無法穿著皮甲以外的盔甲使用盜賊技能。同樣地，德魯伊和牧師也無法使用信仰上不允許的武器。

當你在第一個職業中至少升到第二級後，你就具備了轉換第二種職業的基本資格。條件如同前面所述，你必須符合所有要求，並且不能有任何屬性上的衝突。當你選擇了第二種職業，你的第一種職業就會暫時「冷凍」起來。你將會變成新職業「第一級：經驗點數0」的人物。從此以後，你的人物便依照新職業的規定升級。請注意：一旦轉職，你就再也無法轉回前一個職業。你前一個職業的等級從此固定，永遠不會改變。

在第二個職業的等級超過第一個職業之前，你將無法使用第一個職業的所有能力。舉例來說：如果等級四的法師轉職成戰士，那麼在這個人物成為等級五的戰士前，您都無法利用法師的能力施法。

重要訊息：柏德之門II的經驗點數上限是2900000。而轉職人物兩個職業的經驗點數和也不可超過這個數字。因此，你必須注意人物在轉職後是否有足夠的經驗值可供升級。請注意！若是你原本的職業已經到達等級十四，這代表你第二個職業可能無法到達等級十五，遊戲仍然會容許你轉職，但你可能永遠無法使用第一個職業的技能，這會提高遊戲進行的困難度。除非在資料片中提高了等級的上限。》~

@10851  = ~Minor Spell Turning
(Abjuration)

Level: 5
Range: 0
Duration: 3 rounds/level
Casting Time: 5
Area of Effect: The caster
Saving Throw: None

This spell is similar to the 7th-level Spell Turning, which causes the spells cast against the wizard to rebound upon the original caster. This affects a total of 4 spell levels—including spells cast from scrolls and innate spell-like abilities—but excludes the following: area effects that are not centered directly upon the wizard, as well as area effects that are stationary, such as Cloudkill and Stinking Cloud. As long as the spell is cast directly at the wizard, it will be reflected back upon the caster. This spell will only affect up to 4th-level spells, but as long as there are levels remaining, a spell will be reflected. For example, if there is only 1 level left and a 3rd-level spell is cast at the wizard, the spell will be reflected while canceling the Spell Turning.

This spell will not protect the caster from Dispel Magic, but will not be dispelled by Dispel Magic either.《次級法術反轉（防護系）

等級：5
有效距離：0
持續時間：3輪/每等級
施法時間：5
影響範圍：自身
豁免檢定：無

次級法術反轉和第七級的法術反轉類似，可以將以該法師為目標的法術反彈回初始施法者身上。不過，若反彈的法術等級加總大於4，次級法術反轉便失效。可以反彈的法術包含從卷軸施展的法術，以及具有法術性質的特殊能力，不能反彈的則包含不是以法師為中心施展的區域性法術，以及持續性的區域法術，例如死雲術和臭雲術。只要是直接以該法師為目標的法術，都可以被反彈。不過此法術最高只能反射最高第四級的法術，但只要反彈的法術等級加總仍小於4，次級法術反轉便完全有效。舉例而言，目前反彈的法術等級總計為3，但此時有一個第三級的法術施展於該法師身上，則該等級三的法術被反彈，同時次級法術反轉失效。

@10985  = ~Confusion
(Enchantment/Charm)

Level: 7
Sphere: Chaos
Range: Visual range of the caster
Duration: 1 round/2 levels
Casting Time: 7
Area of Effect: 15-ft. radius
Saving Throw: Neg. 

This spell causes confusion in one or more enemy creatures within the area, creating indecision and the inability to take effective action. All enemy creatures within the area of effect are allowed Saving Throws vs. Spell with a -2 penalty. Those successfully saving are unaffected by the spell. Those who fail their Saving Throws will either go berserk, stand confused, or wander about for the duration of the spell.

The spell lasts for 1 round for every two levels of the caster. Wandering creatures move as far from the caster as possible according to their most typical mode of movement (characters walk, fish swim, bats fly, etc.). Any confused creature that is attacked perceives the attacker as an enemy and acts according to its basic nature.《困惑術（附魔/魅惑系）

等級：7
領域：混亂
有效距離：施法者視野所及
持續時間：1輪/每2等級
施法時間：7
影響範圍：半徑15呎
豁免檢定：通過則無效

此法術會讓影響範圍中一個或以上的生物感到混亂，變得猶疑不覺、不能夠果決地採取行動。所有範圍內的生物均可以-2不利進行對法術的豁免檢定，通過則不受此法術的影響。

施法者每2等級即可使此法術的效果多持續1輪。亂走的生物會盡可能遠離施法者，採用它們最普遍的移動方式（人物行走，魚類游泳、蝙蝠飛走等等）。被困惑的生物一旦遭受攻擊，便會把攻擊者視為敵人，並且依照本性來戰鬥。》~

@10997  = ~Regeneration
(Necromancy)

Level: 7
Sphere: Healing
Range: Touch
Duration: 1 round/2 levels
Casting Time: 7
Area of Effect: 1 creature
Saving Throw: None 

This powerful spell enables the priest to imbue one creature with the ability to regenerate. This regeneration will heal any wounds and even regenerate lost limbs. The creature affected will regain 3 Hit Points per second. The effect lasts for 1 round per 2 levels of the caster or until dispelled. For example, a 14th-level priest would regenerate 18 Hit Points per round for 7 rounds.《再生術（死靈系）

等級：7
領域：醫療
有效距離：觸碰
持續時間：1輪/每2等級
施法時間：7
影響範圍：目標生物
豁免檢定：無

這道強力的法術可賦予受術者再生的能力，受術者的傷勢會自動復原，甚至連殘肢都可以再生。受術者每秒可以恢復3點的生命值，效果可持續1輪/每2等級的時間，或是直到被解除為止。舉例而言，十四級的牧師所施展的再生術，每輪可恢復18點生命值，持續7輪的時間。》~

@11014  = ~Shield of the Archons《亞瓊力場》~
@11015  = ~Shield of the Archons
(Abjuration)

Level: 7
Sphere: Protection
Range: Touch
Duration: 3 rounds/level
Casting Time: 9
Area of Effect: The caster
Saving Throw: None

This powerful abjuration spell causes the spells cast against the priest to be absorbed and consumed. This affects a total of spell levels equal to half the level of the caster. This includes spells cast from scrolls and innate spell-like abilities, but excludes the following: area effects that are not centered directly upon the priest, as well as area effects that are stationary, such as Cloudkill and Stinking Cloud. As long as the spell is cast directly at the priest, it will be absorbed provided that there are spell levels remaining. For example, if there is only 1 level left and a 3rd-level spell is cast at the priest, the spell will be absorbed while canceling the shield.《亞瓊力場（防護系）

等級：7
領域：保護
有效距離：觸碰
持續時間：3輪/每等級
施法時間：9
影響範圍：自身
豁免檢定：無

亞瓊力場是威力強大的防護力場，可以吸收以該法師為目標的法術。不過若吸收的法術等級總計大於牧師等級一半以上，亞瓊力場便會失效。可以吸收的法術包含從卷軸施展的法術，以及具有法術性質的特殊能力，不能吸收的則包含不是以法師為中心施展的區域性法術，以及造成持續性效應的廣域法術，例如死雲術和臭雲術。只要是直接以該法師為目標的法術，都可以被吸收，只要吸收的法術等級總計仍小於牧師等級的一半，亞瓊力場便完全有效。舉例而言，目前尚可吸收的法術等級只剩1級，但此時有一個等級三的法術施展於該牧師身上，則該等級三的法術同樣會被完全吸收，但亞瓊力場的效果也會消失。》~
